CREATE TABLE ADMIN.D_CALENDARS
(
        DAY_KEY DATE NOT NULL,
        RETAILER_WEEK INTEGER NOT NULL,
        FISCAL_WEEK INTEGER NOT NULL,

        FISCAL_YEAR SMALLINT NOT NULL,
        RETAILER_MONTH INTEGER NOT NULL,
        FISCAL_MONTH INTEGER NOT NULL,
        WEEK_ENDING_DATE DATE NOT NULL,
        SHORT_MONTH_NAME CHARACTER VARYING(3) NOT NULL,
        LONG_MONTH_NAME CHARACTER VARYING(9) NOT NULL,
        RETAILER_SEASON_ID CHARACTER VARYING(5) NOT NULL,
        RETAILER_SEASON_NAME CHARACTER VARYING(11) NOT NULL,
        FISCAL_SEASON_ID CHARACTER VARYING(5) NOT NULL,
        FISCAL_SEASON_NAME CHARACTER VARYING(11) NOT NULL,
        FISCAL_QUARTER CHARACTER VARYING(6) NOT NULL,
        RETAILER_QUARTER CHARACTER VARYING(6) NOT NULL,
        RETAILER_QUARTER_DESC CHARACTER VARYING(12) NOT NULL,
        CALENDAR_WEEK INTEGER DEFAULT 0,
        CALENDAR_YEAR SMALLINT DEFAULT 0,
        CALENDAR_MONTH INTEGER DEFAULT 0,
        CALENDAR_SEASON_ID CHARACTER VARYING(5),
        CALENDAR_SEASON_NAME CHARACTER VARYING(11),
        CALENDAR_QUARTER CHARACTER VARYING(6),
        CALENDAR_QUARTER_DESC CHARACTER VARYING(12),
        ACTUAL_YEAR SMALLINT DEFAULT 0,
        ACTUAL_MONTH INTEGER DEFAULT 0,
        ACTUAL_SEASON_ID CHARACTER VARYING(5),
        ACTUAL_SEASON_NAME CHARACTER VARYING(11),
        ACTUAL_QUARTER CHARACTER VARYING(6),
        ACTUAL_QUARTER_DESC CHARACTER VARYING(12),
        SHORT_ACTUAL_NAME CHARACTER VARYING(3),
        LONG_ACTUAL_NAME CHARACTER VARYING(9),
        FISCAL_QUARTER_DESC CHARACTER VARYING(19),
        CAN_RETAILER_WEEK INTEGER DEFAULT 0,
        CAN_FISCAL_WEEK INTEGER DEFAULT 0,
        CAN_RETAILER_YEAR INTEGER DEFAULT 0,
        CAN_FISCAL_YEAR INTEGER DEFAULT 0,
        CAN_RETAILER_MONTH INTEGER DEFAULT 0,
        CAN_FISCAL_MONTH INTEGER DEFAULT 0,
        CAN_RETAILER_SEASON_ID CHARACTER VARYING(5),
        CAN_FISCAL_SEASON_ID CHARACTER VARYING(5),
        CAN_FISCAL_QUARTER CHARACTER VARYING(6),
        CAN_RETAILER_QUARTER CHARACTER VARYING(6),
        DAY_OF_WEEK CHARACTER VARYING(9),
        WEEKEND_FLAG SMALLINT DEFAULT 0,
        DAY_OF_YEAR SMALLINT DEFAULT 0,
        RETAILER_MONTH_445 INTEGER DEFAULT 0,
        RETAILER_MONTH_NAME_445 CHARACTER VARYING(9),
        RETAILER_YEAR_445 SMALLINT DEFAULT 0,
        RETAILER_QUARTER_445 CHARACTER VARYING(6),
        RETAILER_QUARTER_DESC_445 CHARACTER VARYING(12),
        RETAILER_SEASON_ID_445 CHARACTER VARYING(5),
        RETAILER_SEASON_NAME_445 CHARACTER VARYING(11),
        ACTUAL_FISCAL_MONTH INTEGER DEFAULT 0,
        ACTUAL_FISCAL_MONTH_NAME CHARACTER VARYING(9),
        ACTUAL_FISCAL_YEAR SMALLINT DEFAULT 0,
        ACTUAL_FISCAL_QUARTER CHARACTER VARYING(6),
        ACTUAL_FISCAL_QUARTER_DESC CHARACTER VARYING(12),
        ACTUAL_FISCAL_SEASON_ID CHARACTER VARYING(5),
        ACTUAL_FISCAL_SEASON_NAME CHARACTER VARYING(20)
)

CREATE TABLE ADMIN.F_DAILY_GOAL_DETAIL_LOG
(
        DAY_KEY DATE NOT NULL,
        DOOR_KEY CHARACTER VARYING(12) NOT NULL,
        FIELD_REPORTING_KEY CHARACTER VARYING(14) NOT NULL,
        SAP_SHIP_TO_STATE_PROVINCE_KEY CHARACTER VARYING(9) NOT NULL,
        REPORTING_LINE_ID SMALLINT NOT NULL,
        GOAL_LEVEL_TYPE CHARACTER VARYING(1) NOT NULL,
        GOAL_DOLLARS NUMERIC(15,4) NOT NULL DEFAULT '0'::"NUMERIC",
        GOAL_STRETCH_DOLLARS NUMERIC(15,4) NOT NULL DEFAULT '0'::"NUMERIC",
        GOAL_LOCKED SMALLINT NOT NULL DEFAULT 0,
        GOAL_LAST_UPDATED TIMESTAMP NOT NULL DEFAULT '0001-01-01 01:01:00.000000'::"NVARCHAR",
        USER_KEY CHARACTER VARYING(10) NOT NULL,
        DOOR_CLOSE_STATUS CHARACTER VARYING(1) NOT NULL,
        DOOR_CLOSE_DATE DATE NOT NULL DEFAULT '0001-01-01'::"NVARCHAR",
        SAP_CLOSE_REASON_CODE CHARACTER VARYING(3) NOT NULL,
        LOG_USER CHARACTER VARYING(10) NOT NULL,
        LOG_DATE TIMESTAMP NOT NULL DEFAULT '0001-01-01 01:01:00.000000'::"NVARCHAR",
        LOG_MESSAGE CHARACTER VARYING(50) NOT NULL
)
DISTRIBUTE ON RANDOM;


ALTER TABLE ADMIN.F_DAILY_GOAL_DETAIL_LOG
ADD CONSTRAINT F_DAILY_GOAL_DETAIL_LOG_PK
PRIMARY KEY (DAY_KEY, DOOR_KEY, FIELD_REPORTING_KEY, SAP_SHIP_TO_STATE_PROVINCE_KEY, REPORTING_LINE_ID, LOG_DATE);
